    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer6211842245316096340"><b>In the follow-up to Colleen Hoover’s #1 New York Times bestseller <i>Hopeless</i>, the charming and irresistible Dean Holder tells the passionate story that has melted thousands of hearts.</b><br/><br/>In <i>Hopeless</i>, Sky left no secret unearthed, no feeling unshared, and no memory forgotten, but Holder’s past remained a mystery.<br/><br/>Still haunted by the little girl he let walk away, Holder has spent </span>
  <span id="freeText6211842245316096340" style="display:none"><b>In the follow-up to Colleen Hoover’s #1 New York Times bestseller <i>Hopeless</i>, the charming and irresistible Dean Holder tells the passionate story that has melted thousands of hearts.</b><br /><br />In <i>Hopeless</i>, Sky left no secret unearthed, no feeling unshared, and no memory forgotten, but Holder’s past remained a mystery.<br /><br />Still haunted by the little girl he let walk away, Holder has spent his entire life searching for her in an attempt to finally rid himself of the crushing guilt he has felt for years. But he could not have anticipated that the moment they reconnect, even greater remorse would overwhelm him…<br /><br />Sometimes in life, if we wish to move forward, we must first dig deep into our past and make amends. In <i>Losing Hope</i>, bestselling author Colleen Hoover reveals what was going on inside Holder’s head during all those hopeless moments—and whether he can gain the peace he desperately needs.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6211842245316096340" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

You will enjoy all three, as they are meant to be read together!<br />The Colleen Hoover Collection: Hopeless, Losing Hope, and Finding Cinderella (Hopeless #1, 2, 2.5)<br />by Colleen Hoover (Goodreads Author)<br /> 4.75 · Rating Details · 586 Ratings · 11 Reviews<br />Follow four unforgettable characters--Sky and Dean, Daniel and Six--on their journeys to happily ever after in this special collection from #1 New York Times bestselling author Colleen Hoover.<br /><br />HOPELESS<br />When Sky first meets Dean Holder, he both terrifies and intrigues her--and his well-kept secrets may turn out to dismantle her entire life and open the wounds of her own dark past.<br /><br />LOSING HOPE<br />Haunted by the little girl he couldn't save from immediate danger, Holder's life has been overshadowed by guilt, and it is only in loving Sky that he can finally begin to heal himself.<br /><br />FINDING CINDERELLA<br />Daniel's disbelief in love at first sight is stripped away the day he meets Six, a girl with a strange name and an even stranger personality. <span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Yes and no. There are many parts in Losing Hope that are just from Holder's perspective from Hopeless. The story starts about a year before he meets S<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Yes and no. There are many parts in Losing Hope that are just from Holder's perspective from Hopeless. The story starts about a year before he meets Sky and there are some extra scenes as well. I was a little worried about reading it at first because I didn't want to reread the situations, but reading it in Holder's perspective just showed how great he really was. Hope this helps! <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

<div id="review_529400122" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/529400122" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/529400122?book_show_action=true">Feb 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=6-star-books">6-star-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer529400122" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14856776444809423594"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311517i/688486._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> Holy hell. HOLY. HELL.<br/><br/>I can't stop living, breathing and feeling this story. Losing Hope was just absolute, beautiful perfection. </b><br/><br/>I thought I already loved Dean with all my heart, but now I love him more. So. Much. More. I now understand every part of him. Everything he experienced, I went through it with him. The bracelet... finding the letter... needing space... needing her. Finding her. Wow.<br/><br/>I felt this book with every single part of my heart and soul. I swear, it owns a piece of me now.<br/><br/>It. W</span>
  <span id="freeText14856776444809423594" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311517i/688486._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Holy hell. HOLY. HELL.<br><br>I can't stop living, breathing and feeling this story. Losing Hope was just absolute, beautiful perfection. </b><br><br>I thought I already loved Dean with all my heart, but now I love him more. So. Much. More. I now understand every part of him. Everything he experienced, I went through it with him. The bracelet... finding the letter... needing space... needing her. Finding her. Wow.<br><br>I felt this book with every single part of my heart and soul. I swear, it owns a piece of me now.<br><br>It. Was. Perfect.<br><br>So much of Losing Hope is new. It's not just an alternate perspective, it's actually a whole different part of the story entirely. But if you piece it together with Hopeless, you just get EVERYTHING.<br><br>Losing Hope took me through all the same emotions of Hopeless but they were magnified because every single thing that happened now carried the weight of the emotion you already knew from Hopeless PLUS the new emotions created by all the new things we learned in Losing Hope about Holder.<br><br>This is Holder's story. You need to understand just how much I mean those words. This is HIS story. This isn't just Hopeless from Holder's POV, this is his story during Hopeless, his story before Hopeless, and his story apart from Hopeless.<br><br>We see a lot of his past - it's heart breaking and devastating but we live it with him. I went through everything with him. I felt his anger, his loss, his fears. When he fucked up, I cringed. When he was happy, my heart overflowed.<br><br>You know, it's funny 'cuz you think you know a character. I mean, after reading the whole of Hopeless, I really felt like I knew him. But now I'm just realizing that there was so much more going on. And I loved that it didn't change him, just... I guess connected me with him more.<br><br>There were times when I had to just stop and read a single sentence over and over again because it was so beautifully written. There were scenes that gave me full body chills - from head to toe. There were moments where I just closed my eyes and sat there sobbing, letting the emotions sink in.<br><br>I read Losing Hope as slowly as I could because I just didn't want it to ever end. I was WITH the characters every single step of the way. Totally connected. Totally involved. Totally absorbed in every aspect of the story.<br><br><b> I didn't just read this book, I lived it. </b><br><br>I have to say that in all honesty, even though I knew all the twists from reading Hopeless, each one of them hit me as though it was the first time in Losing Hope. Probably because it wasn't as though I was just re-reading them, I was actually re-experiencing them through Holder's eyes. And I loved that there were new twists too - things that were going on with just him personally that took me by surprise in the most wonderful way.<br><br>While so much of this book is just completely new, even the scenes that are the same as in Hopeless feel SO special when you read them because a) they are just awesome scenes to relive period, and b) the slightly different angle on them gives them just enough of a twist to make you fall in love with them all over again.<br><br>Colleen Hoover's talent for writing vivid and effortlessly beautiful stories is astounding. The level of emotions conveyed in each chapter just took my breath away over and over again. She has a gift for bringing everything to life with her words and can write even the simplest scene in such a way that the words just sink right into your heart.<br><br>Pain. Devastation. Love. Loss. Hope. Losing Hope. Finding Hope. Closure. This book has it all.<br><br>When I was finished reading I just sat there hugging my book, letting the emotions sink it, letting the tears flow, and letting myself just FEEL.<br><br>This is a must-read for every fan of Hopeless. It truly completes that story.<br><br>I can't wait for the world to really meet Dean Holder ❤<br><br><b> 6 stars - A must read of 2013! </b><br><br>Release date: July 9, 2013 <br><br><i> ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review. </i><br><br>❤ <u> FAVORITE QUOTES </u> ❤<br><blockquote> <i> <b><br><br>“What are the chances that the only two girls in my life I’ve ever loved… I’ve lost? It’s killing me piece by piece every single day.”<br><br><br><br>“Thirteen years. I’ve been looking for her for thirteen years… I’m not sure that I’m ready for her to remember me yet.”<br><br><br><br>“It’s causing my hands to shake and my heart to pound and my chest to ache because all I want to do is wrap my arms around her and hold her and thank God we finally found each other again.”<br><br><br><br>“If I could trade lives with her I would do it in a heartbeat, just so she’d never have to feel what it is she’s feeling right now.”<br><br><br><br>“I’m scared if I kiss her too soon, it’ll feel like every other kiss she’s ever received. She’ll feel nothing. I don’t want her to feel nothing when I kiss her. I want her to feel everything.”<br><br><br><br>“I let everything I’m seeing sink in because this is what I want to remember the most. I want to remember exactly what she looks like the second she hands over a piece of her heart.”<br><br><br><br>“Fuck all the firsts, Sky. The only thing that matter to me with you are the forevers.”<br><br> </b></i>
</blockquote>   <br><br><br>I'll admit, this is kinda how I'm feeling right now:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/574066.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14856776444809423594" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_529851361" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/529851361" />
    <a title="xrysa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9016476-xrysa"><img alt="xrysa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1438615835p2/9016476.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/529851361?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="xrysa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="xrysa" href="/user/show/9016476-xrysa">xrysa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9016476-xrysa?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9016476-xrysa?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer529851361" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13087554060077977986"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311517ra/688487.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It is really hard for me to review this book since it's one of my favorite books <u>ever.</u>Hopeless and losing hope show us the same events but from differents POVs.In this book we have Holder's POV and I was kind of expecting it to be like the first book but <b>NO</b>.Even though the events are almost the same his book is different and I dont think you will get the feeling of reading the same book.At least that's how I felt.I fell in love again with him and Sky.There were those parts where I knew exactly w</span>
  <span id="freeText13087554060077977986" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311517ra/688487.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It is really hard for me to review this book since it's one of my favorite books <u>ever.</u>Hopeless and losing hope show us the same events but from differents POVs.In this book we have Holder's POV and I was kind of expecting it to be like the first book but <b>NO</b>.Even though the events are almost the same his book is different and I dont think you will get the feeling of reading the same book.At least that's how I felt.I fell in love again with him and Sky.There were those parts where I knew exactly what will happen and yet I cried a river and for this reason I love the author.LOL dont worry I'm not a masochist but the fact that I got the same feelings like I was reading it for the first time means a lot.<br><br><br><b>Holder</b><br><i>It's been years now but every time I look up at the sky I think about her.</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311517i/688488.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Sky</b><br><i>She's the one that will give him hope everyday.</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311517i/688489.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holder's life was never easy.For years he had been accusing himself for Hope's missing but it wasn’t his fault.He was a protective brother and he loved a lot his sister.He always knew that something was off with her as she was spending nights crying in his arms but he did his best to be there and strong for her.However she managed to break him with a selfish decision that she took.<i>She left him <b>alone</b> and <b>hopeless</b></i>.<br><br>A few months after his sister loss he decides to return back to his previous life but he never thought that a trip to the grocery's store would change his life.<br><br> <b><blockquote>My heart stops.</blockquote>
<br> <blockquote>Time stops.</blockquote>
<br> <blockquote>The whole world stops.</blockquote>
<br> <blockquote>I recognize those eyes.</blockquote>
<br> <blockquote>Those are Hope's eyes.</blockquote></b><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688490.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He is not sure if she is his friend but he has to know her, <i>be with her.</i>As it seems they have many things in common and these two are simply the best book couple ever!I laughed a lot with their sarcasm but mostly I loved being in his head.Ughh I remember reading somewhere that he is just a horny teen. Well yeah what do you expect?He's a guy and of course his only purpose was to tease her to hell and have naughty thoughts.I'm glad that Holder is not the perfect guy who would do this skinny love thing.He is outspoken and arrogant.<br><br>Life for these two is full of surprises.If you have read the first book you know what I mean.It hurts him so much that she cant remember him and it's actually devastating reading how he feels .I wanted to hug him so much *sigh*. <br><br><b>I cant protect her from all the memories that are flooding her mind (...)</b><br><br>And then we have the breaking down point.God I felt like I had never read this before , like I didnt know what was coming.I was literary hanging from the words.<br><br><b>I cry for her.I cry for Les.I cry for myself.</b><br><br>These scenes brought to me so many tears.We dont get all the details from Sky's POV and I was so surprised with a few revelations.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311518ra/688491.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Ok,I know it has nothing to do with the review but I feel like writing a letter to Les and to every Les that might read it :)<br><br><br> <i>
  <blockquote>Dear Les ,<br>I know it was hard for you.It broke you to pieces and I'm really sad about it. I'm sure you dont want anyone’s pity so no pities are given.You had been through to so many difficult situations and yet you managed to stay on your feet.You seemed happy.You were smiling .You seemed content but we have now conluded to the fact that you were the best actress. I'm not accusing you for lying, I'd never do that. You were only pretending because you actually cared about the people you loved. You were always the best for this. Unfortunately we are humans and we have boundaries. You were strong enough for so many years but you met your crux point.You couldnt take it anymore and many will blame you for being a coward.On the other hand there is also a handful of people who will think that you were brave to take a decision like this.Sadly,I dont think I belong to either of these groups. You have to know that we admire you for being strong but decisions shouldn’t be shellfish and yours was.Dont take me wrong!I know you fought a lot but you actually left behind you debris and destroyed people.So you that you can relate with Les's story take care and think wisely before you act because there might be someone who really cares about you.<br><br>Be save ,<br>Kristina </blockquote>
</i><br><br>A heartwarming series that had its ups and downs came to the end.I will never forget these characters and I'm really glad I met them. these kind of book should be read by everyone because these are stories of life and love.<br><br><b>She's my saving grace.<br>My Hope,<br>And I'm never walking away from her.</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311518ra/688492.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>I honestly thought I'd always be hopeless but I find hope every single day</b>
</i>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311518ra/688493.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311518ra/688494.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>Arc courtesy of Atria books via NetGallery in exchange of an honest review.</i></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer529361985" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2922316946822166040"><b>5+ Blew me away stars!</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/8ea8a77f-ce78-447b-8771-566f804eb125_zpscb9e1313.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311520i/688566._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo 8ea8a77f-ce78-447b-8771-566f804eb125_zpscb9e1313.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Just when I thought it couldn’t get any better than <i>Hopeless</i>, Colleen Hoover proves me wrong! I loved that <i>Losing Hope</i> wasn’t just <i>Hopeless</i> from Holder’s pov... it was so much more. Dean Holder is just perfection. You get his story from before Hopeless, and during, and those letters. Those letters destroyed me in the very best way. This book was just amazing. Every book I read by this author gets better and better. I don’t know how she does it, I’m just glad that she do</span>
  <span id="freeText2922316946822166040" style="display:none"><b>5+ Blew me away stars!</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/8ea8a77f-ce78-447b-8771-566f804eb125_zpscb9e1313.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311520i/688566._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 8ea8a77f-ce78-447b-8771-566f804eb125_zpscb9e1313.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Just when I thought it couldn’t get any better than <i>Hopeless</i>, Colleen Hoover proves me wrong! I loved that <i>Losing Hope</i> wasn’t just <i>Hopeless</i> from Holder’s pov... it was so much more. Dean Holder is just perfection. You get his story from before Hopeless, and during, and those letters. Those letters destroyed me in the very best way. This book was just amazing. Every book I read by this author gets better and better. I don’t know how she does it, I’m just glad that she does! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/28be44f4-9f6a-4e9b-aa64-0d4f4ea9b5e1_zps37ac169f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311520i/688567.jpg" alt=" photo 28be44f4-9f6a-4e9b-aa64-0d4f4ea9b5e1_zps37ac169f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I always have trouble reviewing books like this. If you’ve read <i>Hopeless</i>, then you already know the bulk of the story. If you haven’t read it- you need too asap. It was one of my top reads last year! I’ll give a quick recap... Dean Holder is back after spending a year away at his dad’s. He lost his sister Les, and he’s trying to deal with that. Les and his childhood best friend, Hope were the only two girls he’s ever loved. Both are gone. Les is gone permanently, and Hope... well, he doesn’t know. <br><b>
  <blockquote>What are the chances that the only two girls in my life I’ve ever loved... I’ve lost? It’s killing me piece by piece every single day.</blockquote>
</b><br>Everything changes when he see’s her. This girl reminds him so much of Hope, its really uncanny. Her name is Sky. There is just something about Sky, he has to know her. OMG one of my favorite things about this book was getting some of the scenes from Holder’s pov... the first almost kiss- wow!<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I’m scared if I kiss her too soon, it’ll feel like every other kiss she’s ever received. She’ll feel nothing. I don’t want her to feel nothing when I kiss her. I want her to feel everything.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/620c2c2b-2860-4c3f-8363-62e177f1e81f_zpsa7722f91.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311520i/688568._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 620c2c2b-2860-4c3f-8363-62e177f1e81f_zpsa7722f91.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>‘Fuck all the firsts, Sky. The only thing that matters to me with you are the forevers.’</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Holder made me swoon and fall in love with him all over again. The more he gets to know Sky, the more he starts to suspect she could be Hope. He’s not sure if he wants her to be. He just wants her to be happy. He just wants her. He is falling for her. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I’m pretty sure its too soon to love her, but shit. She’s got to stop doing and saying these things that make me want to fast forward whatever’s going on between us.<br><br>I’m not falling in love with her piece by piece anymore. I’m falling for the whole girl. Every single piece of her. </blockquote>
</b><br>And finding out the truth from Holder’s pov, watching all the pieces fall into place... even though I knew what was coming, I was captivated. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/cfb4ea89-1bed-4faf-a02b-9544745e067d_zps128a8aaa.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311520i/688569.jpg" alt=" photo cfb4ea89-1bed-4faf-a02b-9544745e067d_zps128a8aaa.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Perfection.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/78c415ee-8c30-4a12-8e3c-416d7036eef0_zps33175202.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311520i/688570._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 78c415ee-8c30-4a12-8e3c-416d7036eef0_zps33175202.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>♥<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/296c340e-aaf7-4a09-83c1-d5677ae39669_zps8d166272.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311520i/688571.jpg" alt=" photo 296c340e-aaf7-4a09-83c1-d5677ae39669_zps8d166272.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Getting this arc, and getting to read this now was like Christmas come early for me. It did not disappoint. Not at all. Anything that was a little unclear during <i>Hopeless</i> got clarified. Holder and Sky are an amazing couple and this story is so well written and so freaking beautiful! Colleen Hoover is seriously talented. She has a way to tell a story like no other. I get sucked into her books- I can’t get enough. And the letters...Those letters were so emotional, they were the best part for me. This book was a work of art, perfection. I am so excited for everyone to read it! Just amazing! <br><br><b>I can honestly say I’ve found the only other person in this world who understands my guilt. The only other person who understands my pain. The only person who accepts that it’s who I am. I used to think the best part of me died with Les, but the best part of me is standing right here in front of me.</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/d1604558-5b49-45f6-aeef-c57bed45852a_zpsf0f6f668.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311520i/688572.jpg" alt=" photo d1604558-5b49-45f6-aeef-c57bed45852a_zpsf0f6f668.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><i>**ARC provided by Atria Books via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review**</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="2922316946822166040" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer530911640" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13811264925516117420"><b> ♥ 5 BRILLIANT, EMOTIONAL, HEARTBREAKING, BEAUTIFUL STARS. ♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688507.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688508.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Colleen Hoover has done it again!</b><br/><br/>Colleen Hoover can do no wrong in my book. I've read and loved each and every single one of her books and they were all brilliant, and <b>Losing Hope</b> was no exception. <b>Hopeless</b> was one of my favorite books of 2012 and reading the story again from Holder's POV made me exactly remember why. <br/><br/><i>***Review contains spoilers for those who haven't read Hopeless yet***</i><br/><br/>In <b>
  <i>Hopeless</i>
</b> Sky told her side of the story, bu</span>
  <span id="freeText13811264925516117420" style="display:none"><b> ♥ 5 BRILLIANT, EMOTIONAL, HEARTBREAKING, BEAUTIFUL STARS. ♥</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688507.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688508.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Colleen Hoover has done it again!</b><br><br>Colleen Hoover can do no wrong in my book. I've read and loved each and every single one of her books and they were all brilliant, and <b>Losing Hope</b> was no exception. <b>Hopeless</b> was one of my favorite books of 2012 and reading the story again from Holder's POV made me exactly remember why. <br><br><i>***Review contains spoilers for those who haven't read Hopeless yet***</i><br><br>In <b>
  <i>Hopeless</i>
</b> Sky told her side of the story, but this time, in <b>
  <i>Losing Hope</i>
</b> we get Holder's sode of the emotional journey...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688509._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holder hasn't had an easy year, to say the least. After his twin sister commited suicide, his whole life has spiraled out of control and he hasn't been truly happy ever since. He feels guilty about what happened with his sister and decide to leave the they lived in with their mother and his moves back in with his dad. After having lived with his father for a year, he returns back home only to be confronted with the last person he could have ever expected. The person, he'd been looking for for the past thirteen years...<br><br><br><b>
  <i>"Time stops.<br><br>My heart stops.<br><br>The whole world stops.<br><br>My quick glance turns into a full-on, unintentional stare.<br><br>I recognize those eyes.<br><br>Those are Hope's eyes."</i>
</b><br><br>When Holder meets Sky, he immediately recognizes the young girl who used to be his best friend Hope, but who disappeared thirteen years ago and who's been missing ever since.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688510._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holder soon befriends Sky and starts to spend more time with her, but Sky herself doesn't seem to have any idea who Holder is. She doesn't remember anything from what happened before she was taken away from her home and family when she was just five years old. The more time they spend together, the more Holder starts to fall in love with the girl Sky is now and the more he wishes that she wouldn't be Hope so that their present won't be affected by the events that happened in the past.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>"I've loved Hope since we were kids.<br><br>But tonight?<br><br>Tonight I fell in love with Sky."</i>
</b><br><br><br>What follows is an emotional journey in which Holder has to decide whether Sky should know the truth about what happend all those years ago or if she's better off without those memories of the past. And if she does find out the truth, how I'll it effect her relationship with Holder? In Losing Hope we find out how Holder struggles with knowing the truth but being unable to confide in anyone about it. It's not an easy journey, but we all know that eventually they do get their much deserved happy ending.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688511._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I was in love with the way you loved me. When you wrapped your arms around me and held me, I knew that no matter what happened with my life you were my home."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688512._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holder and Sky's story is filled with heartbreaking moments and reading their story from Holder's POV didn't make it any less emotional. In fact, Holder's side of the story made me even shed more tears than the Sky's story and a huge reason for that were the letters added thoughout the story. Aal of them but one were written by Holder to his sister Les, but the one that tripped me the most was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the one written by Les herself <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688513.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are so many more wonderful and memorable quotes I highlighted throughout the story and that I could include in my review, but I feel like you should really read it for yourself in order to grasp the true message behind this story and it's powerful words. It's a story about losing hope, being hopeless, but being able to find hope once again in the arms of love...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688514.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311518ra/688515.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>If you've read and loved Hopeless as much as I did, you will <i>not</i> be disappointed by this wonderful re-telling of the story! And if you haven't read this series yet, READ IT! And I promise you won't be disappointed either... </b>
  <br>
  <br>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/530924237?book_show_action=true">Feb 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destini mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destini mia" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia">destini mia</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13742215-destini-mia?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer530924237" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4659171820868895373">**Warning: Spoilers for those who haven't read the first one**<br/>Absolutely <b>breathtaking.</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688497.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>A story about <b>love.<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688498._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Loss.<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688499._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Pain.</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688500.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>And <b>forgiveness.</b> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688501.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Just when I thought it couldn’t get better, Colleen Hoover comes and just knocks it out of the park!<br/><b>Dean Holder</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688502.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Linden Sky Davis</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688503.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Holder still hasn’t forgiven himself from walking away from Hope thirteen years ago. And with Les’ death, he isn’t the same person her used to be. <br/>And then he sees her. <br/>And gets to know her.<br/>And falls in love with her.<br/>There are two sides to e</span>
  <span id="freeText4659171820868895373" style="display:none">**Warning: Spoilers for those who haven't read the first one**<br>Absolutely <b>breathtaking.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688497.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>A story about <b>love.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688498._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Loss.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688499._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Pain.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688500.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And <b>forgiveness.</b> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688501.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Just when I thought it couldn’t get better, Colleen Hoover comes and just knocks it out of the park!<br><b>Dean Holder</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688502.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Linden Sky Davis</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688503.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Holder still hasn’t forgiven himself from walking away from Hope thirteen years ago. And with Les’ death, he isn’t the same person her used to be. <br>And then he sees her. <br>And gets to know her.<br>And falls in love with her.<br>There are two sides to every story.<br>And this is Holder’s. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> My heart stops.<br>Time stops.<br>The whole world stops.<br>I recognize those eyes.<br>Those are Hope’s eyes. </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688504._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Honestly, I knew I was going to like <i>Losing Hope</i>, but I was afraid that it was going to be a lot like <i>Hopeless</i>, and therefore, a little boring. <b>I couldn’t have been more wrong.</b> Yes, some parts were the same but it was also different looking at it from Holder’s POV. <br><br>The writing was phenomenal. The author <i>pulls</i> you in and I was experiencing everything with them like I was right there. I didn't want to put it down for a second. I was hooked. Like, wrap my iPad in ziploc bag and read while I shower, hooked. <br><br>Seeing everything through Holder’s eyes, while sometimes cute and hilarious, was heartbreaking. There was so much <b>guilt</b> and <b>pain.</b> I really <i>felt</i> for him in this book, even more than I did in the first one.<br>His guilt and pain over what happened to Les had me tearing up a few times. I don’t even know how to explain how much I <i>felt</i>, for him and for Les. It’s something you definitely need to experience on your own. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> You knew I would be the one to find you and the fact that you knew that and you still killed yourself?<br>I hated that you did it anyway, knowing you wouldn’t be the only one who died. I was so mad because you let me die, too. </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>And the weight of walking away from Hope… was devastating. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> What are the chances that the only two girls in my life I’ve ever loved… I’ve lost? </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>In <i>Losing Hope</i>, I really began to understand Holder. There were a few times in book one where I would question him but now I really know what went on and how precious Sky was to him. <br>Their relationship was even more beautiful reading it from Holder’s POV. With everything they have been through, they deserved each other. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311518ra/688505.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>If anything would make me believe in soulmates, it would be Holder and Sky.<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “You know how I feel about you,” I whisper, staring into her eyes. “You know how much I love you. You know I would do whatever I could to take away your pain, right?<br>She nods, never pulling her gaze from mine, even for a second.<br>“I need that from you so fucking bad right now, Sky. I need to know you love me like that.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>The series is an <b>absolute must read.</b> You'll fall in love with the characters, the writing, and the story. <br>Just <b>stunning.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688506.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>**ARC courtesy of Atria Books via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review**</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="4659171820868895373" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_652856907" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/652856907" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/652856907?book_show_action=true">Jun 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=cry-baby-books">cry-baby-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer652856907" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13871555967669284606"><b>
  <i>”I love you, Holder. So much,” she says firmly. “And just so you know…so did Hope.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688563.jpg' width='381' height='410' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This story had me thinking from the first chapter what a fan-freaking-tastic read Hopeless would have be if it would have been written in alternating povs! <br/><br/>Seriously, I really enjoyed <i>Hopeless</i> but with the knowledge of Dean Holder’s past, inner most thoughts, his sister Leslie and that ending, the completed story was…perfection. <br/><br/>If you had read my review for <i>Hopeless</i> <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/402907387'>http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/...</a> th</span>
  <span id="freeText13871555967669284606" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>”I love you, Holder. So much,” she says firmly. “And just so you know…so did Hope.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688563.jpg" width="381" height="410" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story had me thinking from the first chapter what a fan-freaking-tastic read Hopeless would have be if it would have been written in alternating povs! <br><br>Seriously, I really enjoyed <i>Hopeless</i> but with the knowledge of Dean Holder’s past, inner most thoughts, his sister Leslie and that ending, the completed story was…perfection. <br><br>If you had read my review for <i>Hopeless</i> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/402907387">http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/...</a> then you’ll get my comparison of the story to a puzzle that came without a box. I thought that it was “complete” by the end of the book but I was wrong. <br> <br>Not until you read <i>Losing Hope</i> can a reader sit back and fully absorb the beauty of the full puzzle.<br><br>Once again, a reader could highlight a majority of the book seeing as Colleen Hoover is a brilliant weaver of words. Don't hate me, but I gave up on two popular books that came out with alternate pov of the same stories. That being said, this is definitely worth the read and I have no regrets.<br> <br>Dean Holder’s pov added several intricate and relevant scenes to story and I can’t think of anything that she could have done more with this book. Even though there are scenes that were the same in this book and the outcome is the same there are additions to even the ending that complete the overall picture.<br><br>Dean’s losses, his frustrations, his grief, his struggle with wanting her to be Hope as well as the fear that she could be Hope…<br><br><b>
  <i>“How can she not remember? How anyone not remember being stolen from her own home? From her best friend? <br>How can she not remember me?”</i>
</b><br><br>Dean falling into live and then love was just swoon worthy...<br><br><b>
  <i>”I can’t even explain to you how perfect this girl is. And when I say perfect, I mean imperfect, because there’s just so much wrong with her. But everything wrong with her is everything that draws me in and makes her perfect.”</i>
</b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m scared if I kiss her too soon, it’ll feel like every other kiss she’s ever received. She’ll feel nothing. I don’t want her to feel nothing when I kiss her. I want her to feel everything.”</i>
</b><br><br>Overall, job well done Colleen Hoover, you are truly a gifted writer. Readers will love Dean's pov and live and love him even more if possible!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311520i/688564.png" width="300" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>**ARC courtesy of Atria Books via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review**</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="13871555967669284606" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1467748148" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1467748148" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1467748148?book_show_action=true">Dec 13, 2015</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476746555" href="/book/show/17571797-losing-hope">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1467748148" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6122685119482166227"><b> 3.75 stars </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “I've loved Hope since we were kids. But tonight? Tonight I fell in love with Sky.” </i> </b><br/><br/>Losing Hope was a book I told myself at the beginning of 2015 that I would read this year. I just didn't realize I'd wait until the year was finally over to read it. But New Year's Resolution partially accomplished! Got a few more books to read to do so.<br/><br/>It's been a while since I read Hopeless, and that went in my favor when reading this book. Because it had been almost 2 years since reading the fir</span>
  <span id="freeText6122685119482166227" style="display:none"><b> 3.75 stars </b><br><br><b> <i> “I've loved Hope since we were kids. But tonight? Tonight I fell in love with Sky.” </i> </b><br><br>Losing Hope was a book I told myself at the beginning of 2015 that I would read this year. I just didn't realize I'd wait until the year was finally over to read it. But New Year's Resolution partially accomplished! Got a few more books to read to do so.<br><br>It's been a while since I read Hopeless, and that went in my favor when reading this book. Because it had been almost 2 years since reading the first book, reading from Holder's point of view was a fresh perspective and didn't feel like a reread of a book I already read. <br><br><b> <i> “All those nights you held me and just let me cry . . . you have no idea how many times you’ve already saved me.” </i> </b><br><br>My favorite part was Holder's letters he wrote, they were an easy way to show what he was thinking without it being entirely inner monologue. I also got to see Hope/Sky through new eyes and view Holder's struggles with his decisions. <br><br>In a way I am sad and glad I waited so long to read this book. Sad because it's really good but glad for reasons stated above, it was like reading something new. I recommend this book to all Colleen Hoover and Hopeless fans, it's a real treat for those who love her books.<br><br><b> <i> "I’ve learned over the past year what it really means to be able to miss someone. In order to miss someone, that means you were privileged enough to have them in your life to begin with.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/RRR.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444273756i/16478167._SX540_.png" alt=" photo RRR.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15073173273085760570">4 Stars<br/><br/><b>“Swoonworthy, Heartbreaking and Lovely”</b><br/><br/>“Losing Hope” is the story of “Hopeless” by Colleen Hoover told from Dean Holder’s perspective.. and yet it is oh so much more. I said earlier (in my review of “Hopeless”) Holder is swoonworthy did I not? Romantic, kind and considerate - he’s the most incredible brother, boyfriend and friend. If this guy was the real deal well, I’d hunt him down already! Baawaahh!!! (Of course I don’t mean it.. I’m more than twice his age but one can pretend.. lol.)<br/><br/>A</span>
  <span id="freeText15073173273085760570" style="display:none">4 Stars<br /><br /><b>“Swoonworthy, Heartbreaking and Lovely”</b><br /><br />“Losing Hope” is the story of “Hopeless” by Colleen Hoover told from Dean Holder’s perspective.. and yet it is oh so much more. I said earlier (in my review of “Hopeless”) Holder is swoonworthy did I not? Romantic, kind and considerate - he’s the most incredible brother, boyfriend and friend. If this guy was the real deal well, I’d hunt him down already! Baawaahh!!! (Of course I don’t mean it.. I’m more than twice his age but one can pretend.. lol.)<br /><br />Anyhow, this novel, should not be missed!! If you loved “Hopeless” - this truly rounds out Holder’s story and just makes you love him more so please check it out.<br /><br />Published on Goodreads on 2.1.20.</span>

  <span id="freeText8834367687489973040" style="display:none"><br><b>5 in the SKY Stars</b><br><br>For more reviews, visit <a href="http://www.jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Jacqueline’s Reads</a>.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/140wUJq" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688547.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>I must warn you, there will be A LOT of hand holding pictures, I just COULD.NOT.HELP.MYSELF!!!</b><br><br>What can I say… I absolutely loved <a>Hopeless </a> and is probably if not my favorite read of all time.<br><br><b>Damn Colleen Hoover, YOU.CAN.WRITE</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/iEB9Mn9" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688548.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Losing Hope</i> is <i>Hopeless</i> from Holder’s POV. Remember the part where Sky and Holder didn’t talk to each other for one month, oh.my.gah…. it was killing me… I wanted to know what Holder was doing, what he was up to, what he was thinking, who he was seeing and YES, Yes, and YES I got it! Thank you!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>I am mad at you Holder… But no matter how mad I’ve been, I never for one second stopped wanting you here with me</i>
</b><br><br>If you kind of liked Holder from <i>Hopeless</i> then you basically want to pin him to the bed and face rape him when you finish <i>Losing Hope</i><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/f8AyR9v" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688549._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>I LOVED HOLDER from <i>Hopeless</i>, but by GOD having Holder’s POV is like drinking a glass of wine… no matter how much you consume… you just want more and get drunk on it</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/pcDneRg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688550.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And… so did Jacqueline (just saying)<br><br>Do not even get me started on the first non-kiss. Oh lord, who knew dry humping and NOT kissing was so freaking hot! I just LOVE IT! I’ll say it again, I LOVE Colleen Hoover’s writing. I want to go into my kitchen right now and force husband to make me dinner, just so I can make-out with him or have him grope me.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/BnhHbeb" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311519ra/688551.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What made <i>Hopeless</i> such a great read was all the dynamics that went on, like Sky unraveling her past and Holder making Sky whole again. Now, what makes <i>Losing Hope</i> such a great read was seeing the inner struggles Holder was dealing with and how he overcame them. I didn’t think he was so abrasive in <i>Hopeless</i>, but damn, when he fights, it’s SEXY!<br><br>Oh and the things that come out of his mouth…<br><br><b>
  <i>You can hold my hand, you can run your fingers through my hair, you can straddle me while I feed you spaghetti, but you are not getting kissed tonight. </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>F&amp;ck all the firsts, Sky. The only thing that matters to me with you are the forevers<i></i></i>
</b><br><br><b>Sheesh… FAINT right here</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/01v55SD" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688552.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>One last thing, I think <i>Hopeless/Losing Hope</i> had one of the most moving, intense and yes BEST sex scene. It wasn’t just steamy, it was just such a vital and pivotal point in the read and I am so glad it was written the way it was written. To this day, I compare that scene to other scenes in my current reads and there is just no comparison.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/8CsmtuP" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688553.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>This isn’t me saying yes, Holder. This is me saying yes</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>You were always there, you know. Even when I couldn’t remember… you were always there</i>
</b><br><br>Despite the first tiny part was a little slow for me, the rest definitely made up for it. If you had any questions about Les and Holder’s relationship, <i>Losing Hope</i> answers that.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/5Rc1QWC" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311519ra/688554.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/sUBXPDc" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688555.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/prxWnN7" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688556.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/VPkBt1m" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_529255592" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/529255592" />
    <a title="*.Amaia.* BlackMagicRose" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14475340-amaia-blackmagicrose"><img alt="*.Amaia.* BlackMagicRose" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435489639p2/14475340.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/529255592?book_show_action=true">Feb 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*.Amaia.* BlackMagicRose" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*.Amaia.* BlackMagicRose" href="/user/show/14475340-amaia-blackmagicrose">*.Amaia.* BlackMagicRose</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">EVERY single person in this freakin' world</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14475340-amaia-blackmagicrose?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14475340-amaia-blackmagicrose?shelf=abuse-mental-disorder-neglect">abuse-mental-disorder-neglect</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14475340-amaia-blackmagicrose?shelf=youngadult-newadult">youngadult-newadult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14475340-amaia-blackmagicrose?shelf=arcs-netgalley">arcs-netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14475340-amaia-blackmagicrose?shelf=his-pov">his-pov</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer529255592" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8208615097689139458"><b>
  <u>**If you haven't read book 1, please, stop reading right now. I don't wanna spoil this amazing story for you :) **</u>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311518ra/688518.gif' width='304' height='91' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>**ARC courtesy of Atria Books via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review**</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688519.jpg' width='400' height='234' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'll be lying if I said this book wasn't the one I was most looking forward to reading this year. It was. And I'm so grateful I got to read this ARC before it was released because I'm sure the wait would have been absolute torture. My expectations were high, and well, this is Colleen Hoover we are talki</span>
  <span id="freeText8208615097689139458" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>**If you haven't read book 1, please, stop reading right now. I don't wanna spoil this amazing story for you :) **</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311518ra/688518.gif" width="304" height="91" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>**ARC courtesy of Atria Books via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review**</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688519.jpg" width="400" height="234" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'll be lying if I said this book wasn't the one I was most looking forward to reading this year. It was. And I'm so grateful I got to read this ARC before it was released because I'm sure the wait would have been absolute torture. My expectations were high, and well, this is Colleen Hoover we are talking about, so I wasn't the least worried. <br><br>Using and adapting some of those perfect words by the author:<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>I've loved <i>Hopeless</i> since I read it back in January. But today? Today I fell in love with <i>Losing Hope</i>.</blockquote>
</b> <br><br>Those of you who have read Hopeless you pretty much know what the story is about and well, why read this book then if all the mistery has been revealed? Let me tell you that <b>there is SO much more to know</b>. This boy/man can still surprise us and melt our hearts. Reading this story again from <b>Holder's POV is a gift and being inside his head is a privilege</b>. <br><br><br>The book starts right before <b>Les, Holder's twin sister, makes a decision that will shatter Holder and his family's life,</b> again. He is <i>the boy who lost Hope</i> and he could never recover himself from that, and now, he is completely broken. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688520.jpg" width="400" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fortunately <b>he meets Sky and discovers that after all, he might not be completely hopeless</b>. She might be the one to put him back together in so many different ways, because she was his past and she now could become his future. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688521.jpg" width="400" height="266" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You all know what comes after that, <b>cute but absolutey hot moments, also completely heartbreaking</b>, that keep you hooked until the very end. And being able to get to know <b>what's in Holder's head in those moments, believe me, it's PRICELESS</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688522.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's painful to read all that <b>guilt and pain</b> from Holder's POV, but it's also so powerful how little by little <b>he starts to heal</b>, the incredible way he expresses his feelings by writing to his sister. It's so totally worth it. It's incredible how a man, a monster, can make so much harm and at the same time create as a consequence such a <b>beautiful and perfect story of two people who are meant to be together, even if for a while, they were forced to be apart</b>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311518ra/688523.gif" width="400" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Once again, this story broke my heart and put it back together, as if it was the first time. So READ it and LOVE it. That's all *.*</b> <br><br> </span>

    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=perfect-book-boyfriend">perfect-book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=cat-heart-these-books">cat-heart-these-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer571705396" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3942438255190564316"><i> <b>“I wonder if it's possible for people to fall in love with a person one characteristic at a time, or if you fall for the entire person at once.” </b></i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688534.jpg' width='300' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Okay, I will not explain the story behind this book because it’s the exactly same one than the first one. If you haven’t read it yet, I advise you to do it faster.<br/>I will only say that this was already an amazing story under Sky’s POV and it was even a greater one under Holder’s. Oh, how I love his mind and the fact that he never actually lose hope. <br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688535.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Us</span>
  <span id="freeText3942438255190564316" style="display:none"><i> <b>“I wonder if it's possible for people to fall in love with a person one characteristic at a time, or if you fall for the entire person at once.” </b></i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688534.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay, I will not explain the story behind this book because it’s the exactly same one than the first one. If you haven’t read it yet, I advise you to do it faster.<br>I will only say that this was already an amazing story under Sky’s POV and it was even a greater one under Holder’s. Oh, how I love his mind and the fact that he never actually lose hope. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688535.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Usually, when I read books under the hero’s POV the girl annoys the hell out of me. I’m happy to say that didn't happen in this one. I liked Sky as much as I in the first book and the connection she and Holder have is one of the amazing things in this book. <br>How he falls in love with Sky, for the girl she is now, and not because she’s Hope, the girl he searches since he was a kid. <br><br><i> <b>“But I'm not falling in love with her piece by piece anymore. I'm in love with the whole girl. Every single piece of her.”</b></i><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311518i/688536._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Although this book was sadder than the first with the entire Les story, it was also better and had the addiction of some great characters (Yes, Daniel!! A book about him would be the greatest thing ever!) <br><br>I really don't know what to say. I loved it. :D<br>I couldn’t get enough of Holder’s mind and if I had one complaint, and it’s just one, I wish a longer epilogue. (Both in time and in length.) <br>If you liked the first, you really can’t miss this one. :)</span>

<div id="review_583641671" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/583641671" />
    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/583641671?book_show_action=true">Apr 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer583641671" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11029293648390576723"><b>♥♥♥ 5 beautiful, Hope-filled stars!!♥♥♥</b><br/><br/>Well, it's official. CoHo has done it again with Losing Hope. Now, I know most you are probably sick of this alternate POV trend as I was. I mean, why not write a book with dual POV in the first place. Anyway, CoHo has written something very insightful about why she wrote Losing Hope on her blog, which you can find <a href='http://colleenhoover.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>here.</a><br/><br/>Now onto our review...<br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/sHx6YKj' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688538.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>In a nutshell, Losing Hope is more than just a retelling of Hopeless. Yes, we know what happened already so why s</span>
  <span id="freeText11029293648390576723" style="display:none"><b>♥♥♥ 5 beautiful, Hope-filled stars!!♥♥♥</b><br><br>Well, it's official. CoHo has done it again with Losing Hope. Now, I know most you are probably sick of this alternate POV trend as I was. I mean, why not write a book with dual POV in the first place. Anyway, CoHo has written something very insightful about why she wrote Losing Hope on her blog, which you can find <a href="http://colleenhoover.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">here.</a><br><br>Now onto our review...<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/sHx6YKj" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688538.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In a nutshell, Losing Hope is more than just a retelling of Hopeless. Yes, we know what happened already so why should we bother reading the same story again? Well, as I mentioned above there is more to it than just retelling the same story in Hopeless. We get to see/read about two new characters, Les and Daniel. Les is not really new but we get to know her a little better here. We also get to know the enigma that is Dean Holder.<br><br>It's been a long time since I've read Hopeless and I have actually forgotten how swoony Holder can be. I swear, if you loved him in Hopeless, you will fall in love with him more in this book, if that's even possible. And you get to see his tortured and wounded side, which was just totally heartbreaking. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/xltiknR" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688539.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In this book, we also get to explore or at least, we get a clearer picture of the relationship between Les and Holder. Gah! Those journal entries had me bawling like a baby. And the fact that Holder poured out his feelings to his sister through that journal was just heartbreaking. And although we pretty much knew what happened to Les, as it was already revealed in Hopeless, reading it again from Holder's POV was just gut-wrenching.<br><br>Plus of course, we really get to see how Holder felt about Sky from the moment he saw her and his developing feelings towards her. Swoon! I mean really, I'm 34 years old but their story still gets to me. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/4OQBkn6" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688540._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/9PaezYV" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688541._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I just love the way CoHo writes her books. There's an honesty and openness, coupled with her effortless prose that makes reading her books easy. Easy in a sense that the story just flows wonderfully, from the highs to the lows, through the conflicts and resolutions without the reader ever feeling duped or short-changed. There are no purple prose here, folks. It's just concise and straightforward writing. Nothing more. And it works every time. It's definitely worth reliving Holder and Sky's story all over again.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/pMtdXU0" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311519i/688542.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>ARC provided by Atria through NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>
